< Text>
Had a great experience shopping for a dishwasher there. Roy the Sales Rep was very courteous, kind, and helpful...great guy and a Vietnam Veteran to boot as we talked Army shop while going through the sales process. Bought my dishwasher and delivery was already on the way to my house as soon as I left Frank's. Just waited at home a few short minutes until delivery arrived. The installation guy (I forgot to get his name) did an excellent job in taking out my old early 90's dishwasher and installing the new Whirlpool stainless steel modern day dishwasher. The installer was kind enough to let me know I had a minor leak in my hot water valve under my sink (I just replaced today in seconds) which he didn't have to do. Installer had no problems or issues installing and was done within an hour, hour and a half. Many thanks to the installer, professional and courteous! Could not get over how quiet the dishwasher sounds when running, Roy the salesman said it was super quiet, he was right! I will DEFINITELY return there for my next replacement appliance.  Kudos to all of you!<//Text>

<Pictures>None<//Pictures><rating>5<//rating>< Text>
I'm glad there's a decent Filipino food restaurant nearby. This place is clean and the people running the place are nice and friendly. The food is priced reasonably and the serving is generous. My personal favorite is the pork sinigang (you can request for extra "sabaw") I have also tried their beef caldereta, pork menudo, and pork kare-kare (surprisingly good as I am used to beef kare-kare). Their lechon kawali is often freshly fried which makes it deliciously crispy. They also sell popular Filipino kakanin. If you're a fan of Filipino food, try this place out... you won't get disappointed.< /Text>

Have been stopping by here for years now... ever since they were at the original location around the corner on Mission before the 6th Street bridge construction. < Text>
I scheduled a check up and a dental cleaning for my rescue kitty, Senor Perry, and I was impressed by Plaza del Amo Animal Hospital. The reception staff was extremely helpful and caring from the moment I entered the clinic. I explained that my cat was semi-feral and needed to be in a quiet place away from barking dogs. He was immediately placed in a quiet room waiting for the doctor.
Dr. Ogino is an incredibly nice, caring human being, very professional and extremely good with cats. She saw how terrified my boy was and even sprayed Feliway in the room to calm him down.
She did a great job with cleaning my kitty's teeth and even took before and after pictures to show me what she did. I did not expect that. She also took ample time afterwards to explain the blood tests in great detail, advising me how to care best for my senior boy in the future. In my 15+ years of animal rescue, I can honestly say Dr. Ogino is one of the most honest and caring doctors I have ever met, delivering a great quality of care for my boy.

I will definitely come to Plaza Del Amo again and bring my kittens here as well. Thanks Lisa, for running this great hospital and showing so much care for Senor Perry and the other furry patients.<//Text>

<Rating>5< /Rating>< Text>
We have boarded our dog, Muna, there with Pet Keepers several times, and he has LOVED staying with them every time. I can tell because every time we go back, he greets the caregivers with enthusiasm, wagging his tail, leaning against their legs, and sitting on their feet, his way of expressing affection (not to mention lots of kisses, if they will let him). This enthusiasm extends to the medical care staff as well: recently we had to deal with a persistent bout of abdominal upset probably triggered by stress and a water and diet change from our move from the desert to the South Bay. The staff were very caring with Muna, caring and gentle, reassuring and careful to explain everything to me. The vet, Dr. Moeller, took extra time to sit down with me and discuss all the options for possible diagnoses from best to worst case scenarios, and different testing and treatment strategies. They gave me the information I needed to make informed decisions, and allowed me to make the best decisions I could afford given all the factors in our lives. I am happy to say that thanks to their care, Muna has returned to his normal bouncy good health, and in spite of his advanced age, we're looking forward to several more years with our happy, healthy dog!</Text>

<review>White Horse is a really great place to visit for delicious New Orleans Cajun. The food and drinks are very well priced for the outstanding quality you get, and the servers and bartenders are extremely knowledgeable as well. Feel safe when visiting, everything is being done with the COVID best practice requirements. Great happy hour offerings as well, especially for those that like 'Old Fashioneds'. I really liked and appreciated the old school music and old fashioned dim bar surroundings, it really was refreshing. The dark wood and red upholstery The exterior design is very tasteful and catches your attention when passing by. The set up works great for those looking for a group setting or even just for couples. I found the brunch menu to be especially enticing, I'm going to need to come back a couple of times to try out all the things that looked promising. The parking structure is right next door for maximum convenience. This place is truly a hidden gem amongst all the other great places in Pasadena. I'm also looking forward to checking out their sister location, Craft Hill, which I've heard great things about. Brandon was an amazing team member and recommended the fried chicken sandwich, which was fantastic. He knew all the items on the menu almost from memory and went above and beyond to walk me through everything. I'm glad I went with his recommendations. He also told me some cool things to do in the area and South Pasadena, so I have those on my list as well. They don't skip on the portions either, you'll definitely satisfy your appetite and probably have some leftovers as well. I can't think of much they can do to improve things, everything was so great! I plan on visiting again sooner rather than later.<//review><pics>None</pics>< Response>

< user_name>
James Wan< /user_name>
<time>1583312770688<//time>< Text>
A packed dining room and bar put this place quite in the limelight as you enter on a weekend evening. Unfortunately, there were far too many misses to honestly click on an extra star for the rating.

The bar seriously needs to pay attention to customers. Waiting for my party and waiting at the bar, and trying to get a drink was an impossible 5 minutes. They were treating me like I just came out of an AA meeting.

The menu seems to hit most of the notes for a hungry patron. At first glance, you can see it is well designed. Something for everyone wraps the context of each category. Fine Wagyu meats, a great burger, your standard salmon dish, and an attractive Southern Fried Chicken.

Dig deeper and you can find the pretentiousness of certain items. The use of Wagyu in smoked brisket, for example, is quite a redundancy. Why pay for a Wagyu priced cut that is supposed to be slow-smoked/cooked?

The Jumbalaya Rissoto is in fact not "risotto," and made with orzo pasta. Granted it is stated in the description as orzo, the title is completely misleading. If a person was gluten intolerant this would be a horrific experience. This dish is totally not worthy of the $26 price tag for a pasta dish.

The service felt like the servers were really working hard. I overheard a waiter mumbling about covering 8 large tables. I commend the service timing for everyone at the table.

The drinks here are very good. The bar certainly displays some craft behind their creations. I would return for their happy hour, and possibly a revisit for a sample of other items.

I do miss Cheval Blanc that once took this location to new heights in french cuisine.</Text>

< text>
What a wonderful surprise!! The White Horse Lounge is a great place for family, out of town guest spot, romantic two or just friends! The food is an explosion of flavors and mouth watering treats! I kind you not.. the southern fried chicken is seasoned to delight, the Hoe cake made me moooan, the salmon avec haricot verts satisfies the palate with lightness.. and the drinks..well let's just say they don't hold back! The ambiance is Nu Oleans almost classic brothel style with elegant private cubbies tucked aside; it's warm and welcoming and smooth music playing in the background will catch you for a recognizable song.. the service is exceptional, making sure you're delighted to be there. The chef is to be applauded..my understanding is he's been there about a year and a half and he's for sure making a statement at the White Horse Lounge! Oh and did I mention the Blackberry peach cobbler!! The place is high on my list you won't be disappointed!!< /text>
